    WHEN [r].[RecipeID] IS NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, [r].[RecipeID], COALESCE([r].[RecipeName], CASE
    WHEN [m].[MaterialID] IS NOT NULL THEN [m].[MaterialName]
    ELSE N'Unknown Recipe'
END), [r].[BatchSize], CASE
    WHEN [m].[MaterialID] IS NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, [m].[MaterialName], CASE
    WHEN [u].[UomID] IS NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, [u].[UomName], [a].[UserID], [m].[MaterialID], [u].[UomID], [p0].[BatchID], [p0].[BatchNumber], [p0].[Status], [t].[OrderBomId], [t].[MaterialId], [t].[RequiredQuantity], [t].[DispensingStatus], [t].[MaterialName], [t].[MaterialCode], [t].[UomName], [t].[MaterialID0], [t].[UomID], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [ProductionOrderBom] AS [p2]
        WHERE [p].[OrderID] = [p2].[OrderId] AND [p2].[DispensingStatus] <> N'Dispensed') THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END
FROM [ProductionOrders] AS [p]
LEFT JOIN [AppUsers] AS [a] ON [p].[CreatedBy] = [a].[UserID]
LEFT JOIN [Recipes] AS [r] ON [p].[RecipeID] = [r].[RecipeID]
LEFT JOIN [Materials] AS [m] ON [r].[MaterialID] = [m].[MaterialID]
LEFT JOIN [UnitOfMeasure] AS [u] ON [m].[BaseUomID] = [u].[UomID]
LEFT JOIN [ProductionBatches] AS [p0] ON [p].[OrderID] = [p0].[OrderID]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p1].[OrderBomId], [p1].[MaterialId], [p1].[RequiredQuantity], [p1].[DispensingStatus], CASE
        WHEN [m0].[MaterialID] IS NOT NULL THEN [m0].[MaterialName]
        ELSE N'Unknown'
    END AS [MaterialName], CASE
        WHEN [m0].[MaterialID] IS NOT NULL THEN [m0].[MaterialCode]
        ELSE ''
    END AS [MaterialCode], CASE
        WHEN [u0].[UomID] IS NOT NULL THEN [u0].[UomName]
        ELSE N'N/A'
    END AS [UomName], [m0].[MaterialID] AS [MaterialID0], [u0].[UomID], [p1].[OrderId]
    FROM [ProductionOrderBom] AS [p1]
    LEFT JOIN [Materials] AS [m0] ON [p1].[MaterialId] = [m0].[MaterialID]
    LEFT JOIN [UnitOfMeasure] AS [u0] ON [p1].[UomId] = [u0].[UomID]
) AS [t] ON [p].[OrderID] = [t].[OrderId]
ORDER BY [p].[OrderID], [a].[UserID], [r].[RecipeID], [m].[MaterialID], [u].[UomID], [p0].[BatchID], [t].[OrderBomId], [t].[MaterialID0]

    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)

    ELSE N'Unknown Recipe'
END), [r].[BatchSize], CASE
    WHEN [m].[MaterialID] IS NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, [m].[MaterialName], CASE
    WHEN [u].[UomID] IS NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, [u].[UomName], [a].[UserID], [m].[MaterialID], [u].[UomID], [p0].[BatchID], [p0].[BatchNumber], [p0].[Status], [t].[OrderBomId], [t].[MaterialId], [t].[RequiredQuantity], [t].[DispensingStatus], [t].[MaterialName], [t].[MaterialCode], [t].[UomName], [t].[MaterialID0], [t].[UomID], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [ProductionOrderBom] AS [p2]
        WHERE [p].[OrderID] = [p2].[OrderId] AND [p2].[DispensingStatus] <> N'Dispensed') THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END
FROM [ProductionOrders] AS [p]
LEFT JOIN [AppUsers] AS [a] ON [p].[CreatedBy] = [a].[UserID]
LEFT JOIN [Recipes] AS [r] ON [p].[RecipeID] = [r].[RecipeID]
LEFT JOIN [Materials] AS [m] ON [r].[MaterialID] = [m].[MaterialID]
LEFT JOIN [UnitOfMeasure] AS [u] ON [m].[BaseUomID] = [u].[UomID]
LEFT JOIN [ProductionBatches] AS [p0] ON [p].[OrderID] = [p0].[OrderID]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p1].[OrderBomId], [p1].[MaterialId], [p1].[RequiredQuantity], [p1].[DispensingStatus], CASE
        WHEN [m0].[MaterialID] IS NOT NULL THEN [m0].[MaterialName]
        ELSE N'Unknown'
    END AS [MaterialName], CASE
        WHEN [m0].[MaterialID] IS NOT NULL THEN [m0].[MaterialCode]
        ELSE ''
    END AS [MaterialCode], CASE
        WHEN [u0].[UomID] IS NOT NULL THEN [u0].[UomName]
        ELSE N'N/A'
    END AS [UomName], [m0].[MaterialID] AS [MaterialID0], [u0].[UomID], [p1].[OrderId]
    FROM [ProductionOrderBom] AS [p1]
    LEFT JOIN [Materials] AS [m0] ON [p1].[MaterialId] = [m0].[MaterialID]
    LEFT JOIN [UnitOfMeasure] AS [u0] ON [p1].[UomId] = [u0].[UomID]
) AS [t] ON [p].[OrderID] = [t].[OrderId]
ORDER BY [p].[OrderID], [a].[UserID], [r].[RecipeID], [m].[MaterialID], [u].[UomID], [p0].[BatchID], [t].[OrderBomId], [t].[MaterialID0]

SELECT [p].[OrderID], [p].[OrderCode], [p].[RecipeID], [p].[PlannedQuantity], [p].[ActualQuantity], [p].[Status], [p].[StartDate], [p].[EndDate], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[CreatedBy], [a].[FullName], CASE
    WHEN [r].[RecipeID] IS NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, [r].[RecipeID], COALESCE([r].[RecipeName], CASE
    WHEN [m].[MaterialID] IS NOT NULL THEN [m].[MaterialName]
    ELSE N'Unknown Recipe'
END), [r].[BatchSize], CASE
    WHEN [m].[MaterialID] IS NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, [m].[MaterialName], CASE
    WHEN [u].[UomID] IS NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, [u].[UomName], [a].[UserID], [m].[MaterialID], [u].[UomID], [p0].[BatchID], [p0].[BatchNumber], [p0].[Status], [t].[OrderBomId], [t].[MaterialId], [t].[RequiredQuantity], [t].[DispensingStatus], [t].[MaterialName], [t].[MaterialCode], [t].[UomName], [t].[MaterialID0], [t].[UomID], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [ProductionOrderBom] AS [p2]
        WHERE [p].[OrderID] = [p2].[OrderId] AND [p2].[DispensingStatus] <> N'Dispensed') THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END
FROM [ProductionOrders] AS [p]
LEFT JOIN [AppUsers] AS [a] ON [p].[CreatedBy] = [a].[UserID]
LEFT JOIN [Recipes] AS [r] ON [p].[RecipeID] = [r].[RecipeID]
LEFT JOIN [Materials] AS [m] ON [r].[MaterialID] = [m].[MaterialID]
LEFT JOIN [UnitOfMeasure] AS [u] ON [m].[BaseUomID] = [u].[UomID]
LEFT JOIN [ProductionBatches] AS [p0] ON [p].[OrderID] = [p0].[OrderID]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p1].[OrderBomId], [p1].[MaterialId], [p1].[RequiredQuantity], [p1].[DispensingStatus], CASE
        WHEN [m0].[MaterialID] IS NOT NULL THEN [m0].[MaterialName]
        ELSE N'Unknown'
    END AS [MaterialName], CASE
        WHEN [m0].[MaterialID] IS NOT NULL THEN [m0].[MaterialCode]
        ELSE ''
    END AS [MaterialCode], CASE
        WHEN [u0].[UomID] IS NOT NULL THEN [u0].[UomName]
        ELSE N'N/A'
    END AS [UomName], [m0].[MaterialID] AS [MaterialID0], [u0].[UomID], [p1].[OrderId]
    FROM [ProductionOrderBom] AS [p1]
    LEFT JOIN [Materials] AS [m0] ON [p1].[MaterialId] = [m0].[MaterialID]
    LEFT JOIN [UnitOfMeasure] AS [u0] ON [p1].[UomId] = [u0].[UomID]
) AS [t] ON [p].[OrderID] = [t].[OrderId]
ORDER BY [p].[OrderID], [a].[UserID], [r].[RecipeID], [m].[MaterialID], [u].[UomID], [p0].[BatchID], [t].[OrderBomId], [t].[MaterialID0]

    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)

        FROM [ProductionOrderBom] AS [p2]

    WHEN [m].[MaterialID] IS NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)

    WHEN [u].[UomID] IS NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)

        SELECT 1
        FROM [ProductionOrderBom] AS [p2]
        WHERE [p].[OrderID] = [p2].[OrderId] AND [p2].[DispensingStatus] <> N'Dispensed') THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END

        ELSE N'Unknown'

) AS [t] ON [p].[OrderID] = [t].[OrderId]

        FROM [ProductionOrderBom] AS [p2]
        WHERE [p].[OrderID] = [p2].[OrderId] AND [p2].[DispensingStatus] <> N'Dispensed') THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END

    END AS [UomName], [m0].[MaterialID] AS [MaterialID0], [u0].[UomID], [p1].[OrderId]

    LEFT JOIN [UnitOfMeasure] AS [u0] ON [p1].[UomId] = [u0].[UomID]
) AS [t] ON [p].[OrderID] = [t].[OrderId]
